 a post is going viral on social media claiming that Article 30 of the Constitution of India allows madrasas to teach the Quran but Article 30 (A) says that the Gita cannot be taught in schools
 is post se aisa lagata he ki bharat kaa samvidhan dharmik kitaaben padhaane ke bare main bhedbhaavpurn he
 The anti-fake News War Room of India Today found in its investigation that there is no provision in the Constitution including Article 30 (A) which prohibits teaching of Gita
 post kaa archive varjanayahandekha ja saktaa he
 This is going viral on the postfacebook and twitter which reads, "article 30: Quran can be taught in madrasa! Article 30 (A): Gita cannot be read in schools! The credit goes to Jawaharlal Nehru
 ”is daawey kii pushti ke liye hamane samvidhan main is artical kii padtaal kii to paaya ki samvidhan main 30(A) kaa koi astitv hi nahin he
 Article 30 of the Constitution is sub article 30 (1A)
 kya kahata he artical 30?bhartiya samvidhan kaartical 30alpsankhyak virgon ke liye shaikshik sansthaanon kii sthapana karne or uske sanchaalan ke bare main he
 Article 30 (1) states that all minority classes based on religion or language will have the right to establish and administer educational institutions of their interest
 artical 30(1A) kisi alpsankhyak-varg dwaara sthapit or prashasit shiksha sanstha kii sampatti ke anivaary arjan ko sunishchit karata he
 Article 30 (2) states that the State shall not discriminate against any educational institution in assisting educational institutions on the basis that it is under the management of a minority class based on religion or language
 kya kehete hai visheshgy?india today ne is sambandh main loksabhaa ke purv mahasachiv pediti acharya se baat kii
 He said that there is no provision in the Constitution of India about teaching religious books
 hamaara samvidhan dharmanirpeksh he or isamen aisa koi praavdhaan hi nahin he ki madrasa main quran padhaayaa ja saktaa he or skulon main gita nahin padhai ja sakati
 It is clear that there is no provision under Article 30 of the Constitution which makes provision for teaching Gita or Quran in schools
